    <h1>TV Schedule &amp; Episode Calendar</h1>

  <div class="submenu">
    <div class="marea">
      <div class="col_75" style="margin-bottom: 15px;"> 
        <h6><a href="show-select">Quick Filter - Add shows to favourites - View most popular shows</a></h6> 
        <p><a href="show-select">View the full list of popular shows on The TV Calendar and add them to your favourites filter</a></p>
        <p>Note: &quot;The&quot; isn&apos;t treated as part of a show name; e.g. &quot;The Simpsons&quot; is found under &quot;S&quot;</p>  
      </div>

      <div class="col_24" style="text-align: center;"> 
       <form action="disablefilter.php" method="post">

    </div>
      <div class="col_1">
